Curated bibliography of distance sampling publications

Distance sampling applications and theory

Below please find >1500 citations to scientific publications relevant to distance sampling. Many are applications of distance sampling to estimate animal abundance; some are papers describing the development of statistical methods relevant to distance sampling.

Please contact Tiago Marques (tiago.marques@st-andrews.ac.uk) for adding, removing, or correcting entries. Also very welcome are links to existing or to new references.

References
